[CREATURE:WC_WICKER_BEAST]
	[DESCRIPTION:A quadrupedal construct, made from wood, twigs and bone. It has a skull for a head, which is covered with a small wooden mask inscribed with magical symbols. It has two pairs of antlers and two pairs of tusks. An eerie, bluish glow permeates from the slits in its mask and out of the holes in its body. It is animated by a vengeful, feral spirit, and attacks the enemies of its creators. Others of its kind may be found in the wilderness, bereft of purpose, and behaving in a manner similar to predatory animals.]
